  <script type="text/javascript">
   function openMenu()
    {
      if($("#cbp-spmenu-s1").hasClass("cbp-spmenu-open"))
      {
        $("#cbp-spmenu-s1").removeClass("cbp-spmenu-open");
        $("body").removeClass("cbp-spmenu-push-toright");
      }
      else
      {
        $("#cbp-spmenu-s1").addClass("cbp-spmenu-open");
        $("body").addClass("cbp-spmenu-push-toright");
      }
      var getLeft=$(".stick_menu").css("left");
      if(getLeft=="0px")
      {
        $(".stick_menu").css("left","96px");
      }
      else
      {
        $(".stick_menu").css("left","0px");
      }  
    }
  </script>

        <script>
         GCurrentUrl = window.location.href ;
	GCurrentUrl = replaceAll(".loggedin.1","",GCurrentUrl);
	GCurrentUrl = replaceAll(".RegLogout.1","",GCurrentUrl);
	GCurrentUrl = GCurrentUrl.replace(window.location.hash,"");
  // Logout 
  function Logout() {
    document.cookie="usernamepassword=;Path=/;expires=;";
    document.cookie="UserRegID=;Path=/;expires=;";
    document.cookie="LoggedIn=;Path=/;expires=;";
    document.location="/apps/pbcs.dll/frontpage?RegLogout=1";
  }
	// this function needs jquery.js
	function LoginNow(AForm)
	{
		$.ajax(
		{
			type: 'POST',
			data: { 
				login: "1", 
				cookiename: "usernamepassword", 
				email: AForm.Loginemail.value, 
				pwd: AForm.Loginpwd.value, 
				RedirectURL: '/misc/misc/sessioninfo.pbs&Nocache=1&mime=xml&d=' + (new Date()).getTime() 
			},
			url: '/apps/pbcs.dll/reguser?All=1' ,
			success: function(data){
				var LxmlDoc = data || "no response text";
				try
				{
					var LReguser    = LxmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("reguser")[0].childNodes[0].nodeValue;
					if(LReguser != 'null')
						document.location = GCurrentUrl + "&loggedin=1";
					else
						alert("Invalid e-mail address or password");
				}
				catch(err)
				{
					alert("Invalid e-mail address or password");
				}
			},
			error: function(){ console.log('Something went wrong...') }
		});
	}
	function LoginFacebookNow(AType){
		LFacebook = 'https://www.facebook.com/dialog/oauth?client_id=103101790033337&scope=email&redirect_uri=';
		if(AType == 1)
			LRedirect = 'https://www.khaleejtimes.com' + ((GCurrentUrl.toLowerCase()).replace(("https://khaleejtimes.com").toLowerCase(),"")).replace(("https://www.khaleejtimes.com").toLowerCase(),"");
		else
			LRedirect = 'https://www.khaleejtimes.com/';	
		if(CheckUrlForSpecificString('register.ref'))
			LRedirect = 'https://www.khaleejtimes.com' + GetUrlParameter('ref');
		document.location = LFacebook + encodeURIComponent(LRedirect) + "%26loggedin%3D1&extauth=facebook";
	}
	function replaceAll(find, replace, str) {
		return str.replace(new RegExp(find, 'g'), replace);
	}
  function getCookie(name) {
    var dc = document.cookie;
    var prefix = name + "=";
    var begin = dc.indexOf("; " + prefix);
    if (begin == -1) {
        begin = dc.indexOf(prefix);
        if (begin != 0) return null;
    }
    else
    {
        begin += 2;
        var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", begin);
        if (end == -1) {
        end = dc.length;
        }
    }
    return unescape(dc.substring(begin + prefix.length, end));
  } 
  function setCookie(c_name,value,expiredays)
  {                          
     var exdate=new Date();
     exdate.setTime(exdate.getTime() + (expiredays*1000));
     domain_name_part =document.location.host;
     domain_name = domain_name_part.slice(2);
     document.cookie=c_name+ "=" +escape(value)+ ((expiredays==null) ? "" : ";expires="+exdate.toGMTString()+";domain=."+domain_name+";path=/");
  }
  // get url parameter
  function GetUrlParameter(AName)
	{
		AName = AName.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
		var LRegexS = "[\\?&]"+AName+"=([^&#]*)";
		var LRegex = new RegExp( LRegexS );
		var LResults = LRegex.exec( window.location.href );
		if( LResults == null )
			return "";
		else
			return LResults[1];
	}
  // Check Url For Specific String
  function CheckUrlForSpecificString(AString)
  {
    var LUrl = String(window.location);
    if (LUrl.search(AString) != -1) 
      return true;
    else
      return false;
  }
  if (CheckUrlForSpecificString('loggedin') || CheckUrlForSpecificString('userverify') || (getCookie("LoggedIn") != '' && getCookie("LoggedIn") != null))
  {  
    $.ajax(

      url: '/misc/misc/sessioninfo.pbs&Nocache=1&mime=xml&d=' + (new Date()).getTime() ,

          var LUserfname      = LxmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("userfname")[0].childNodes[0].nodeValue;
          var LUserlname      = LxmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("userlname")[0].childNodes[0].nodeValue;
          // custom per user
          var LExtraPhoto     = LxmlDoc.getElementsByTagName("extra_photourl")[0].childNodes[0].nodeValue;

          if(LReguser != 'null')

            	window.location = (window.location.href).replace("&loggedin=1","");
          }
        }

        }

  }

  <script>
   var menuLeft = document.getElementById( 'cbp-spmenu-s1' ),
      menuRight = document.getElementById( 'cbp-spmenu-s2' ),
      menuTop = document.getElementById( 'cbp-spmenu-s3' ),
      menuBottom = document.getElementById( 'cbp-spmenu-s4' ),
      showLeft = document.getElementById( 'showLeft' ),
      showRight = document.getElementById( 'showRight' ),
      showTop = document.getElementById( 'showTop' ),
      showBottom = document.getElementById( 'showBottom' ),
      showLeftPush = document.getElementById( 'showLeftPush' ),
      showRightPush = document.getElementById( 'showRightPush' ),
      body = document.body;
      showLeft.onclick = function() {
        classie.toggle( this, 'active' );
        classie.toggle( menuLeft, 'cbp-spmenu-open' );
        disableOther( 'showLeft' );
      };
      showRight.onclick = function() {
        classie.toggle( this, 'active' );
        classie.toggle( menuRight, 'cbp-spmenu-open' );
        disableOther( 'showRight' );
      };
      showTop.onclick = function() {
        classie.toggle( this, 'active' );
        classie.toggle( menuTop, 'cbp-spmenu-open' );
        disableOther( 'showTop' );
      };
      showBottom.onclick = function() {
        classie.toggle( this, 'active' );
        classie.toggle( menuBottom, 'cbp-spmenu-open' );
        disableOther( 'showBottom' );
      };
      showLeftPush.onclick = function() {
        var getLeft=$(".stick_menu").css("left");
        if(getLeft=="0px"){
          $(".stick_menu").css("left","96px");
        }else{
          $(".stick_menu").css("left","0px");
        }
        classie.toggle( this, 'active' );
        classie.toggle( body, 'cbp-spmenu-push-toright' );
        classie.toggle( menuLeft, 'cbp-spmenu-open' );
        disableOther( 'showLeftPush' );    
      };
      function disableOther( button ) 
      {
        if( button !== 'showLeft' ) {
          classie.toggle( showLeft, 'disabled' );
        }
        if( button !== 'showRight' ) {
          classie.toggle( showRight, 'disabled' );
        }
        if( button !== 'showTop' ) {
          classie.toggle( showTop, 'disabled' );
        }
        if( button !== 'showBottom' ) {
          classie.toggle( showBottom, 'disabled' );
        }
        if( button !== 'showLeftPush' ) {
          classie.toggle( showLeftPush, 'disabled' );
        }
        if( button !== 'showRightPush' ) {
          classie.toggle( showRightPush, 'disabled' );
        }
      }
  </script>
